<h5> <span class="mw-headline" id="For_Flute.2C_Violin.2C_Cello_and_Piano_.28Hummel.29">For Flute, Violin, Cello and Piano (Hummel)</span></h5>
<div class="we"><div id="IMSLP93497" class="we_file_first we_fileblock_11">
